4.0

RANDOMIZATION PROCEDURES

A signed HHS 310 Form, a copy of the institution's IRB-approved informed consent
document, and  written justification for any changes made to the informed consent
for this protocol must be on file at the ECOG Coordinating Center before an ECOG
institution may enter patients. The signed HHS 310, institution’s informed consent,
and  investigator's  justification  for  changes  will  be  submitted  to  the  following
address:

ECOG Coordinating Center
Frontier Science
Attn:  IRB
303 Boylston Street
Brookline, MA   02146-7648
FAX (617) 632-2990

Patients must not start protocol treatment prior to randomization.  Treatment should
start within three working days after randomization.

Steroids will not be permitted on Arm B.

Infusaports  should  not  be  used  for  IL-2  administration  or
continuous IV hydration as this may create an unacceptable infection
risk;

Patients  should  discontinue  any  antihypertensive  therapy  at  least  24
hours prior to initiating each cycle of biochemotherapy. 

. Cisplatin,  vinblastine  and 

interferon  will  only  be  administered

Missed time of the IL-2 infusion will not be made up.
Missed interferon, cisplatin or vinblastine doses should be given if
hypotension resolves within 6 hours of scheduled dosing, otherwise
they should be omitted for that particular treatment day. 

All  dose  reductions  in  IL-2  and  IFN  are  permanent.

Call the SWOG Operations Office at (210) 677-8808 within 24 hours of any
suspected  adverse  event  deemed  either  drug-related,  or  possibly  drug-
related.

Within 10 days the investigator must send the completed (original) Adverse
Reaction (ADR) Form for Investigational Drugs (#391 RF) to the NCI or the
FDA Form #3500 is (for regimens using only commercial agents) to the NCI:

ADR Program

14980 Omicron Dr.
San Antonio, TX  78245-3217

Within  5  working  days  the  investigator  must  send  the  original  Adverse
Reaction  (ADR)  form  for  investigational  drugs  (#391  RF)  or  the  FDA  3500
(Medwatch) for regimens using only commercial agents to:

In addition, CALGB members must telephone the
CALGB Central Office (773-702-9860) within 24 hours of the adverse event as
outlined in Section 5.21.  The CALGB Regulatory Affairs Coordinator will
immediately notify the ECOG Coordinating Center.

Toxicity will be graded according to the Common Toxicity criteria listed in Appendix II.

excluded 

Patients on Arm B should have their antihypertensive medicines held starting  24
hours  prior  to  the  administration  of  IL-2.    Antihypertensive  medicines  can  be
resumed on day 5 or as needed.

Pre-treatment  steroids  (as  antiemetics)  should  not  be  administered  to
patients on Arm B.

A Randomized Phase III Trial of Concurrent Biochemotherapy with Cisplatin, Vinblastine, Dacarbazine,  IL-2 and

APPENDIX II

COMMON TOXICITY CRITERIA

$
0$
0$

•  Fever felt to be caused by drug allergy should be coded as allergy.
•  Fever due to infection is coded under infection only.

•  Urinary tract infection should be coded under infection, not GU.
•  Hematuria resulting from thrombocytopenia should be coded under hemorrhage, not GU.

$

#

#

•  Viral Hepatitis should be coded as infection rather than liver toxicity.

• Pneumonia is considered infection and not graded as pulmonary toxicity unless felt to be resultant from pulmonary changes directly induced by
  treatment.
